                       <div data-reactid="688">
                        <div data-reactid="689">
                         Need to be close to ICE District, Downtown, Commonwealth, Shaw Conference, and Northlands? Don't want to break your budget? Our studio is your cup of tea then! Perched high above Jasper Avenue with some of the best River Valley views in the city.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="690">
                         Fully furnished, upgraded, 670 sqft (62.3 m2) studio in an older, but clean concrete building directly next to Downtown Edmonton. Large 125 sqft (11.6 m2) terrace is perfect for watching the activity down on Jasper Avenue or on the North Saskatchewan River. Suite comes with FREE parking: 1 underground secured parking + very large visitor parking lot. Very few buildings in Central Edmonton offer this level of free parking. Kitchen offers beautiful stainless steel appliances and is fully equipped. Appliances: fridge, stove, dishwasher, microwave, toaster oven, and Tassimo brewing system. Other: pots, pans, plates, cups, cutlery, cutting boards, oven mitts, can opener, and wine opener, and more! Full sized queen bed with memory foam mattress. Top quality sanitary mattress cover for your comfort. High quality sheets always changed and ready for your arrival. 4 soft and fluffy pillows waiting for your head at the end of the day. Other extras: ironing board + iron, Vidal Sassoon hair dryer, and alarm clock. Primary entertainment is provided by high-speed unlimited WiFi. Connected to the WiFi is a 40" Samsung Smart TV with complimentary access to Netflix!
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="691">
                         Conveniently located right next door to Downtown, this neighbourhood is a historical and walkable neighbourhood! Rough around the edges, up-and-coming, and safe are a few descriptors - hipsters, homeless, young professionals, seniors - all very typical of any central area. Easy access to many walking trails with a beautiful river valley location. Amazing ammenities less than 2.0 km away! Stadium LRT Station: 1.0 km **Quarters LRT Station: 1.0 km **Royal Alberta Museum/Chinatown: 1.1 km Little Italy: 1.1 km Commonwealth Stadium: 1.2 km Shaw Conference Centre: 1.3 km **ICE District/Rogers Place: 1.5 km DT Core/City Centre Mall: 1.7 km Northlands EXPO Centre: 1.9 km ** = under construction
                        </div>

                      <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="2018">
                       <div data-reactid="2019">
                        <div data-reactid="2020">
                         Cute and cosy home with comfy beds located in the heart of Ritchie, near trendy Whyte Ave. and beautiful Mill Creek Ravine. The Mosaic Room is close to nightlife, public transport, parks, and the city centre, being located in one of Edmonton's top 3 neighbourhoods. You'll love the tree-lined streets and quiet, friendly atmosphere. The fenced yard has mature trees and a swing and the bathroom has waterfall shower head and a soaker bathtub.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2021">
                         There is one bedroom with a double bed, and a recently renovated full bathroom in the basement. The stairs to the basement are carpeted, but they are steeper than most stairs, so the space may not be ideal for older adults or people with mobility issues. There is a twin bed in the basement, but it does not have its own room.
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="2022">
                         Ritchie is a beautiful neighbourhood with tree-lined streets. There is a music/restaurant venue and a brew pub nearby, as well as a convenience store. Mill Creek Ravine, with its gravel and paved walking paths and bicycle trails, is a few blocks away.
                        </div>
